  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=6.9)
    While the story avoids many AI-writing pitfalls, there are moments of overly formal phrasing and some unnecessarily complex sentence structures that slightly undermine authenticity. The concept of communicating with a monster through light patterns feels fresh, but certain phrases like "the deep-earth sensors registered a shift" read as somewhat generic. The metaphors are generally original, though the "iron to a magnet" simile is conventional. The story does maintain consistent tone and creates a unique scenario that avoids predictable patterns, but occasionally relies on abstract rather than concrete details.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=7.6)

However, phrases like "luminous doubt" recur without variation, and some descriptions ("a scream woven from mathematics and despair") employ unnecessarily elaborate language that feels slightly performative rather than authentic. The narrative maintains consistent tone throughout but occasionally slips into overly ornate phrasing that detracts from its otherwise original premise.

The balance between ornate prose and thematic urgency mostly works, though "molten sarcasm" conceits occasionally strain under weight of message.

  * grade_story_99.txt (grade=6.5)
    Borders on purple prose with "tapestry of lost legends" tropes; telekinesis-as-bookbinding connection feels underexplored despite original premise.

  * grade_story_92.txt (grade=7.0)
    Occasional overwriting ("color bleeds from day into night") clashes with effective details; subverts horror tropes by making the haunting a metaphor for social inequality but leans on haunted mansion clichés without reinvention.

  * grade_story_93.txt (grade=7.1)
    The fractal calling cards and chaotic radio signal subvert tech-thriller tropes with mathematical poetics, but sections revert to clichéd emotional touchstones (e.g., elevator door farewells). Some phrasing (“untamed flow,” “sacred geometry”) veers toward familiar mysticism rather than distinct conceptual innovation.

  * grade_story_94.txt (grade=7.8)
    Original premise with evocative metaphors; occasionally lapses into ornate phrasing ("gravity of desires" over-explained) and emotionally stated rather than embodied grief.

  * grade_story_98.txt (grade=1.9)
    Overly ornate prose borders on purple. Repetition of "woven," "threads," and "patterns" suggests formulaic expression. Sudden internal logic shifts (ruler → tapestry) lack human complexity. The "forgotten ruler" ending is a predictable archetype.

  * grade_story_91.txt (grade=8.8)
    Distinguishes itself through unique conceptualization of weather control; avoids genre clichés with biomechanical aesthetics but occasionally leans on familiar "lone synthetic being" trope with minimal psychological nuance.

  * grade_story_95.txt (grade=8.2)
    The premise avoids tropes, but some phrasing (“crashing crescendo,” “profound wordless song”) risks melodrama. Fairy-tale references are inventive yet unevenly unpacked. Emotional nuance arises in Anselm’s tactile connection to objects but is undercut by over-explaining his epiphany.

  * grade_story_96.txt (grade=7.3)
    Originality shines in the "brimming cup" as non-literal concept, but some elements veer toward fantastical tropes (enchanted objects, witch settings). The "static uniqueness" of the map offers a fresh metaphysical mechanism, but execution occasionally relies on overly ornate descriptions.
